# <a name="supported-metrics-with-azure-monitor"></a><span data-ttu-id="b0517-103">Stöds mått med Azure-Monitor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b0517-103">Supported metrics with Azure Monitor</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="b0517-104">Azure-Monitor finns flera sätt att interagera med statistik, inklusive diagram dem i portalen, komma åt dem via REST API eller fråga dem med PowerShell eller CLI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b0517-104">Azure Monitor provides several ways to interact with metrics, including charting them in the portal, accessing them through the REST API, or querying them using PowerShell or CLI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b0517-105">Nedan finns en fullständig lista över alla just nu med Azure-Monitor mått pipeline.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b0517-105">Below is a complete list of all metrics currently available with Azure Monitor's metric pipeline.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="b0517-106">Andra mått kan finnas i portalen eller med äldre API: er.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b0517-106">Other metrics may be available in the portal or using legacy APIs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b0517-107">Listan innehåller endast tillgängliga med förhandsversion av konsoliderade Azure-Monitor mått pipeline förhandsversion mått.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b0517-107">This list only includes public preview metrics available using the public preview of the consolidated Azure Monitor metric pipeline.</span></span>
>
>
